\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{agl_8py_source_l04412}04412\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\#\ name\ "{}A."{}\ Also\ omitted\ is\ "{}ffi,"{}\ because\ AGL\ maps\ this\ to\ the}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{agl_8py_source_l04414}04414\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\#\ it\ into\ the\ following\ sequence\ of\ three\ UVs:\ U+0066,\ U+0066,\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{agl_8py_source_l04415}04415\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\#\ U+0069.\ The\ name\ "{}arrowvertex"{}\ has\ been\ omitted\ because\ this\ glyph}}
